637→\t\t\t\t\tos.Setenv(key, value)\n   638→\t\t\t\t}\n   639→\t\t\t}()\n   640→\n   641→\t\t\t// read the input config file into equivalent envs\n   642→\t\t\tenvs := readYAMLIntoEnv(t, path)\n 674→\t\treq = httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://example.com/foo\", nil)\n   675→\t\tw   = httptest.NewRecorder()\n   676→\t)\n   677→\n   678→\tcfg.ServeHTTP(w, req)\n   679→\n   680→\tresp := w.Result()\n   681→\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n   682→\n   683→\tbody, _ := ioutil.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n   684→\n   685→\tassert.Equal(t, http.StatusOK, resp.StatusCode)\n   686→\tassert.NotEmpty(t, body)\n   687→}\n   688→\n   689→// readyYAMLIntoEnv parses the file provided at path as YAML.\n   690→// It walks the keys and values and builds up a set of environment variables\n   691→// compatible with viper's expectations for automatic env capability.\n   692→func readYAMLIntoEnv(t *testing.T, path string) [][2]string {\n   693→\tt.Helper()\n   694→\n   695→\tconfigFile, err := os.ReadFile(path)\n   696→\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n   697→\n   698→\tvar config map[any]any\n   699→\terr = yaml.Unmarshal(configFile, &config)\n   700→\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n   701→\n   702→\treturn getEnvVars(\"flipt\", config)\n   703→}\n   704→\n   705→func getEnvVars(prefix string, v map[any]any) (vals [][2]string) {\n   706→\tfor key, value := range v {\n   707→\t\tswitch v := value.(type) {\n   708→\t\tcase map[any]any:\n   709→\t\t\tvals = append(vals, getEnvVars(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s_%v\", prefix, key), v)...)\n   710→\t\tdefault:\n   711→\t\t\tvals = append(vals, *testing.T) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tcfg = defaultConfig()\n\t\treq = httptest.NewRequest(\"GET\", \"http://example.com/foo\", nil)\n\t\tw   = httptest.NewRecorder()\n\t)\n\n\tcfg.ServeHTTP(w, req)\n\n\tresp := w.Result()\n\tdefer resp.Body.Close()\n\n\tbody, _ := ioutil.ReadAll(resp.Body)\n\n\tassert.Equal(t, http.StatusOK, resp.StatusCode)\n\tassert.NotEmpty(t, body)\n}\n\n// readyYAMLIntoEnv parses the file provided at path as YAML.\n// It walks the keys and values and builds up a set of environment variables\n// compatible with viper's expectations for automatic env capability.\nfunc readYAMLIntoEnv(t *testing.T, path string) [][2]string {\n\tt.Helper()\n\n\tconfigFile, err := os.ReadFile(path)\n\trequire.NoError(t, err)\n\n\tvar config map[any]any\n\terr =
